Transcript and translation by
Lutias Kokopelli.

The translation provided on this page is meant to stay as close to the original Japanese text as can be, even if it means sacrificing readability. If you wish instead to enjoy a translation that truly reads like a proper novel, then another translation, less accurate but far more enjoyable, is under the works on my tumblr.

Warning: The original novel adds furigana to every single kanji, all throughout the story. For laziness and priority management reasons, I did not finish adding the furigana yet, and it is unlikely that I will anytime soon. Any kanji which is intended to have an unusual reading has had its furigana specified; any kanji shown in this transcript that does not come with furigana is meant to have its usual reading(s).
